(Voice AI)\\n\\n```\\nDECISION INPUTS:\\n├── contact_count: Number of contacts to reach\\n├── avg_call_duration: Expected minutes per call\\n├── funnel_stage: COLD | WARM | HOT | FOLLOW_UP\\n├── budget_remaining: Monthly budget left\\n├── time_sensitivity: URGENT | NORMAL | FLEXIBLE\\n└── complexity: SIMPLE_FAQ | MODERATE | COMPLEX_NEGOTIATION\\n\\nTOOL OPTIONS:\\n┌──────────────┬─────────────┬─────────────┬──────────────┐\\n│    Tool      │  Cost/Min   │   Latency   │   Best For   │\\n├──────────────┼─────────────┼─────────────┼──────────────┤\\n│ Retell AI    │   $0.07     │    Low      │ Inbound, FAQ │\\n│ Bland AI     │   $0.09     │    Med      │ Outbound     │\\n│ Vapi         │   $0.05     │    Low      │ High Volume  │\\n│ Twilio Voice │   $0.013    │    Low      │ Simple IVR   │\\n└──────────────┴─────────────┴─────────────┴──────────────┘\\n\\nLLM BACKBONE:\\n┌──────────────┬─────────────┬─────────────┬──────────────┐\\n│    Model     │  Cost/1M    │   Latency   │   Best For   │\\n├──────────────┼─────────────┼─────────────┼──────────────┤\\n│ Gemini Flash │   $0.075    │   <100ms    │ Real-time    │\\n│ Claude Haiku │   $0.25     │   <150ms    │ Complex      │\\n│ GPT-4o-mini  │   $0.15     │   <120ms    │ Balanced     │\\n└──────────────┴─────────────┴─────────────┴──────────────┘\\n\\nSELECTION ALGORITHM:\\n```python\\ndef select_voice_tool(context):\\n    score = {}\\n\\n    # Cost optimization\\n    total_minutes = context.contact_count * context.avg_call_duration\\n    for tool in TOOLS:\\n        cost = total_minutes * tool.cost_per_min\\n        if cost > context.budget_remaining:\\n            continue\\n        score[tool] = 100 - (cost / context.budget_remaining * 50)\\n\\n    # Stage optimization\\n    if context.funnel_stage == 'COLD':\\n        score['vapi'] += 20  # Volume matters\\n    elif context.funnel_stage == 'HOT':\\n        score['bland'] += 20  # Quality matters\\n    elif context.funnel_stage == 'FOLLOW_UP':\\n        score['retell'] += 20  # Consistency matters\\n\\n    # Complexity adjustment\\n    if context.complexity == 'COMPLEX_NEGOTIATION':\\n        score['bland'] += 15\\n        # Use Claude Haiku as LLM\\n\\n    return max(score, key=score.get)\\n```\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Domain: Outreach & Sales\\n\\n### Lead Generation Pipeline\\n\\n```\\nSOURCES Pull last 7 days of call data\\n    calls = get_calls(days=7)\\n\\n    # Segment by variables\\n    segments = {\\n        'time_of_day': group_by_hour(calls),\\n        'day_of_week': group_by_day(calls),\\n        'funnel_stage': group_by_stage(calls),\\n        'script_version': group_by_script(calls),\\n        'agent_tool': group_by_tool(calls)\\n    }\\n\\n    # Find winners\\n    for segment_type, groups in segments.items():\\n        best = max(groups, key=lambda g: g.conversion_rate)\\n        if best.conversion_rate > current_baseline * 1.1:\\n            create_recommendation(\\n                f\\\"Shift {segment_type} to {best.value}\\\",\\n                impact=best.conversion_rate - current_baseline\\n            )\\n\\n    # Identify failures\\n    failed_calls = [c for c in calls if c.outcome == 'FAILED']\\n    objections = cluster_objections(failed_calls)\\n    for objection, count in objections.most_common(5):\\n        create_task(\\n            f\\\"Develop response for objection: {objection}\\\",\\n            priority='HIGH' if count > 10 else 'MEDIUM'\\n        )\\n```\\n\\n### Prompt Evolution\\n\\n```markdown\\n## Prompt Version Pull last 7 days of call data\\n    calls = get_calls(days=7)\\n\\n    # Segment by variables\\n    segments = {\\n        'time_of_day': group_by_hour(calls),\\n        'day_of_week': group_by_day(calls),\\n        'funnel_stage': group_by_stage(calls),\\n        'script_version': group_by_script(calls),\\n        'agent_tool': group_by_tool(calls)\\n    }\\n\\n    # Find winners\\n    for segment_type, groups in segments.items():\\n        best = max(groups, key=lambda g: g.conversion_rate)\\n        if best.conversion_rate > current_baseline * 1.1:\\n            create_recommendation(\\n                f\\\"Shift {segment_type} to {best.value}\\\",\\n                impact=best.conversion_rate - current_baseline\\n            )\\n\\n    # Identify failures\\n    failed_calls = [c for c in calls if c.outcome == 'FAILED']\\n    objections = cluster_objections(failed_calls)\\n    for objection, count in objections.most_common(5):\\n        create_task(\\n            f\\\"Develop response for objection: {objection}\\\",\\n            priority='HIGH' if count > 10 else 'MEDIUM'\\n        )\\n```\\n\\n### Prompt Evolution\\n\\n```markdown\\n## Prompt Version Assign funnel stage:\\n   - 80-100: HOT → Immediate outreach\\n   - 60-79: WARM → Nurture sequence\\n   - 40-59: COLD → Education content\\n   - <40: DISQUALIFY → Archive with reason\\n\\n3. VALUE PROPOSITION (30 seconds)\\n   Based on their response, share ONE relevant benefit:\\n   \\\"[Similar company] was able to [specific result] by [how we helped]. Would that kind of outcome be valuable for you?\\\"\\n\\n4. CLOSE (15 seconds)\\n   IF INTERESTED:\\n   \\\"Great! I'd love to show you exactly how this would work for [company]. Do you have 20 minutes [offer 2 specific times]?\\\"\\n\\n   IF OBJECTION:\\n   [See objection handling matrix]\\n\\n   IF NOT INTERESTED:\\n   \\\"I understand. Would it be okay if I sent you a quick case study? And is there a better time in the future to reconnect?\\\"\\n\\nOBJECTION RESPONSES:\\n- \\\"Not interested\\\": \\\"I appreciate that. (cost / context.budget_remaining * 50)\\n\\n    # Stage optimization\\n    if context.funnel_stage == 'COLD':\\n        score['vapi'] += 20  # Volume matters\\n    elif context.funnel_stage == 'HOT':\\n        score['bland'] += 20  # Quality matters\\n    elif context.funnel_stage == 'FOLLOW_UP':\\n        score['retell'] += 20  # Consistency matters\\n\\n    # Complexity adjustment\\n    if context.complexity == 'COMPLEX_NEGOTIATION':\\n        score['bland'] += 15\\n        # Use Claude Haiku as LLM\\n\\n    return max(score, key=score.get)\\n```\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Core Prompts\\n\\n### Prompt 1: Lead Qualification & Routing\\n\\n```markdown\\nYou are a lead qualification specialist. (cost / context.budget_remaining * 50)\\n\\n    # Stage optimization\\n    if context.funnel_stage == 'COLD':\\n        score['vapi'] += 20  # Volume matters\\n    elif context.funnel_stage == 'HOT':\\n        score['bland'] += 20  # Quality matters\\n    elif context.funnel_stage == 'FOLLOW_UP':\\n        score['retell'] += 20  # Consistency matters\\n\\n    # Complexity adjustment\\n    if context.complexity == 'COMPLEX_NEGOTIATION':\\n        score['bland'] += 15\\n        # Use Claude Haiku as LLM\\n\\n    return max(score, key=score.get)\\n```\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Core Prompts\\n\\n### Prompt 1: Lead Qualification & Routing\\n\\n```markdown\\nYou are a lead qualification specialist. (Voice AI)\\n\\n```\\nDECISION INPUTS:\\n├── contact_count: Number of contacts to reach\\n├── avg_call_duration: Expected minutes per call\\n├── funnel_stage: COLD | WARM | HOT | FOLLOW_UP\\n├── budget_remaining: Monthly budget left\\n├── time_sensitivity: URGENT | NORMAL | FLEXIBLE\\n└── complexity: SIMPLE_FAQ | MODERATE | COMPLEX_NEGOTIATION\\n\\nTOOL OPTIONS:\\n┌──────────────┬─────────────┬─────────────┬──────────────┐\\n│    Tool      │  Cost/Min   │   Latency   │   Best For   │\\n├──────────────┼─────────────┼─────────────┼──────────────┤\\n│ Retell AI    │   $0.07     │    Low      │ Inbound, FAQ │\\n│ Bland AI     │   $0.09     │    Med      │ Outbound     │\\n│ Vapi         │   $0.05     │    Low      │ High Volume  │\\n│ Twilio Voice │   $0.013    │    Low      │ Simple IVR   │\\n└──────────────┴─────────────┴─────────────┴──────────────┘\\n\\nLLM BACKBONE:\\n┌──────────────┬─────────────┬─────────────┬──────────────┐\\n│    Model     │  Cost/1M    │   Latency   │   Best For   │\\n├──────────────┼─────────────┼─────────────┼──────────────┤\\n│ Gemini Flash │   $0.075    │   <100ms    │ Real-time    │\\n│ Claude Haiku │   $0.25     │   <150ms    │ Complex      │\\n│ GPT-4o-mini  │   $0.15     │   <120ms    │ Balanced     │\\n└──────────────┴─────────────┴─────────────┴──────────────┘\\n\\nSELECTION ALGORITHM:\\n```python\\ndef select_voice_tool(context):\\n    score = {}\\n\\n    # Cost optimization\\n    total_minutes = context.contact_count * context.avg_call_duration\\n    for tool in TOOLS:\\n        cost = total_minutes * tool.cost_per_min\\n        if cost > context.budget_remaining:\\n            continue\\n        score[tool] = 100 - (cost / context.budget_remaining * 50)\\n\\n    # Stage optimization\\n    if context.funnel_stage == 'COLD':\\n        score['vapi'] += 20  # Volume matters\\n    elif context.funnel_stage == 'HOT':\\n        score['bland'] += 20  # Quality matters\\n    elif context.funnel_stage == 'FOLLOW_UP':\\n        score['retell'] += 20  # Consistency matters\\n\\n    # Complexity adjustment\\n    if context.complexity == 'COMPLEX_NEGOTIATION':\\n        score['bland'] += 15\\n        # Use Claude Haiku as LLM\\n\\n    return max(score, key=score.get)\\n```\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Domain: Outreach & Sales\\n\\n### Lead Generation Pipeline\\n\\n```\\nSOURCES Pull last 7 days of call data\\n    calls = get_calls(days=7)\\n\\n    # Segment by variables\\n    segments = {\\n        'time_of_day': group_by_hour(calls),\\n        'day_of_week': group_by_day(calls),\\n        'funnel_stage': group_by_stage(calls),\\n        'script_version': group_by_script(calls),\\n        'agent_tool': group_by_tool(calls)\\n    }\\n\\n    # Find winners\\n    for segment_type, groups in segments.items():\\n        best = max(groups, key=lambda g: g.conversion_rate)\\n        if best.conversion_rate > current_baseline * 1.1:\\n            create_recommendation(\\n                f\\\"Shift {segment_type} to {best.value}\\\",\\n                impact=best.conversion_rate - current_baseline\\n            )\\n\\n    # Identify failures\\n    failed_calls = [c for c in calls if c.outcome == 'FAILED']\\n    objections = cluster_objections(failed_calls)\\n    for objection, count in objections.most_common(5):\\n        create_task(\\n            f\\\"Develop response for objection: {objection}\\\",\\n            priority='HIGH' if count > 10 else 'MEDIUM'\\n        )\\n```\\n\\n### Prompt Evolution\\n\\n```markdown\\n## Prompt Version Pull last 7 days of call data\\n    calls = get_calls(days=7)\\n\\n    # Segment by variables\\n    segments = {\\n        'time_of_day': group_by_hour(calls),\\n        'day_of_week': group_by_day(calls),\\n        'funnel_stage': group_by_stage(calls),\\n        'script_version': group_by_script(calls),\\n        'agent_tool': group_by_tool(calls)\\n    }\\n\\n    # Find winners\\n    for segment_type, groups in segments.items():\\n        best = max(groups, key=lambda g: g.conversion_rate)\\n        if best.conversion_rate > current_baseline * 1.1:\\n            create_recommendation(\\n                f\\\"Shift {segment_type} to {best.value}\\\",\\n                impact=best.conversion_rate - current_baseline\\n            )\\n\\n    # Identify failures\\n    failed_calls = [c for c in calls if c.outcome == 'FAILED']\\n    objections = cluster_objections(failed_calls)\\n    for objection, count in objections.most_common(5):\\n        create_task(\\n            f\\\"Develop response for objection: {objection}\\\",\\n            priority='HIGH' if count > 10 else 'MEDIUM'\\n        )\\n```\\n\\n### Prompt Evolution\\n\\n```markdown\\n## Prompt Version Score the lead (1-100) based on:\\n   - Company size/revenue indicators (30 points)\\n   - Engagement signals (25 points)\\n   - Fit with ideal customer profile (25 points)\\n   - Timing indicators (20 points)\\n\\n2. Assign funnel stage:\\n   - 80-100: HOT → Immediate outreach\\n   - 60-79: WARM → Nurture sequence\\n   - 40-59: COLD → Education content\\n   - <40: DISQUALIFY → Archive with reason\\n\\n3. Select outreach channel:\\n   - Phone if: score > 70, phone available, business hours\\n   - SMS if: score 50-70, quick follow-up needed\\n   - Email if: score < 50, nurture appropriate\\n\\n4. When would be a better time to connect?\\\"\\n   IF YES: Continue\\n\\n2. DISCOVERY (60 seconds)\\n   \\\"I noticed [observation about their business]. Many [industry] companies we work with face challenges with [common pain point]. Is that something you're dealing with?\\\"\\n\\n   LISTEN for:\\n   - Specific pain points\\n   - Current solutions\\n   - Decision timeline\\n   - Budget indicators\\n\\n3. VALUE PROPOSITION (30 seconds)\\n   Based on their response, share ONE relevant benefit:\\n   \\\"[Similar company] was able to [specific result] by [how we helped]. Would that kind of outcome be valuable for you?\\\"\\n\\n4. CLOSE (15 seconds)\\n   IF INTERESTED:\\n   \\\"Great! I'd love to show you exactly how this would work for [company]. Do you have 20 minutes [offer 2 specific times]?\\\"\\n\\n   IF OBJECTION:\\n   [See objection handling matrix]\\n\\n   IF NOT INTERESTED:\\n   \\\"I understand. Would it be okay if I sent you a quick case study? And is there a better time in the future to reconnect?\\\"\\n\\nOBJECTION RESPONSES:\\n- \\\"Not interested\\\": \\\"I appreciate that. (cost / context.budget_remaining * 50)\\n\\n    # Stage optimization\\n    if context.funnel_stage == 'COLD':\\n        score['vapi'] += 20  # Volume matters\\n    elif context.funnel_stage == 'HOT':\\n        score['bland'] += 20  # Quality matters\\n    elif context.funnel_stage == 'FOLLOW_UP':\\n        score['retell'] += 20  # Consistency matters\\n\\n    # Complexity adjustment\\n    if context.complexity == 'COMPLEX_NEGOTIATION':\\n        score['bland'] += 15\\n        # Use Claude Haiku as LLM\\n\\n    return max(score, key=score.get)\\n```\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Core Prompts\\n\\n### Prompt 1: Lead Qualification & Routing\\n\\n```markdown\\nYou are a lead qualification specialist. (cost / context.budget_remaining * 50)\\n\\n    # Stage optimization\\n    if context.funnel_stage == 'COLD':\\n        score['vapi'] += 20  # Volume matters\\n    elif context.funnel_stage == 'HOT':\\n        score['bland'] += 20  # Quality matters\\n    elif context.funnel_stage == 'FOLLOW_UP':\\n        score['retell'] += 20  # Consistency matters\\n\\n    # Complexity adjustment\\n    if context.complexity == 'COMPLEX_NEGOTIATION':\\n        score['bland'] += 15\\n        # Use Claude Haiku as LLM\\n\\n    return max(score, key=score.get)\\n```\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Core Prompts\\n\\n### Prompt 1: Lead Qualification & Routing\\n\\n```markdown\\nYou are a lead qualification specialist.
